 somvaar ko vah andolankaaree mahila sanghathanon se mili
 Special Works Officer (OSD) Ranjan Mukherjee said, "khanna voluntarily returned to the city last night
 unhen kendriya grih mantralay kii ore se bulaayaa nahin gaya he
 On reaching here, he met women's organizations and assured them to take all necessary steps for the safety of women
 " On Monday, two Assistant Commissioners of Delhi Police were reprimanded and suspended for not stopping the operation of buses with curtained windows amidst criticism for the lapse in security arrangements
 uparajyapal khanna ne bataaya ki dilli yatayaat police ke mohan singh dabaas or police control room ke ram singh ko nilambit kar diya gaya
 Three policemen have already been suspended
 udhar, bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) ke saansadon kaa pratinidhimandal mangalvaar ko raashtrapati pranab mukherjee se mulaakaat kar unase sansad kaa vishesh satr bulaane kii maang karegaa, taaki dushkarm kii ghatnaon ko rokane ke liye sakht kanoon banaaya ja sake
 The comments bhaajapa netaa sushamaa swaraj ne sanvadaataaon se kaha, "ham unase anurodh karenge ki vah sarkaar ko sansad kaa vishesh satr bulaane ke liye kahen
 " ullekhneey he ki dushkarm kii badhati ghatnaon ke kaaran dilli ko 'dushkarm kii rajdhani' kaha jane laga he
 Police figures show that there have been more than 600 rape cases in Delhi this year
 rashtriya rajdhani par lage is daag ko dhonaa ab centre or dilli sarkaar ke liye chunauti ban gai he
 Describing Janakrosh's performance as 'just and trustworthy anger and anguish', Manmohan Singh said that he has felt the pain of gang rape as a father of three daughters
 unhone kaha ki aparaadh par gussa karnaa 'nyaaysangat' he lekin hinsa se koi uddeshy puraa nahin hoga
 Just before the Prime Minister's statement came, the victim's father pleaded for peace on the news channels and asked people to pray for his daughter, who is in critical condition in a hospital
 pahchaan chhipaane ke liye televijan par unka cheharaa haalanki dhundhala kar diya gaya tha
 Manmohan Singh said, "I myself have felt this incident as a father of three daughters, as every one of you has felt
 meri patni, meraa parivaar or main, sabhi krurtapurna aparaadh se peedit yuvati ke liye kii ja rahi chintaa main shaamil hai
 We are constantly monitoring his condition
 aaie, ham sabhi is mahatvapurn samay main uske liye or uske mitra ke liye prarthana karen
 " pradhanmantri ne kaha, "ham na keval is bhayanak aparaadh ke babat avilamb jaanch karenge, balki mahilaon or bacchon kii suraksha se sambandhit sabhi pahaluon par vichaar karenge or jo log aise rakshasi aparaadhon ko anjaam diya he unhen dandit karenge
 Our government will give you information about all the steps and procedures being taken in this direction

" " It is noteworthy that due to the increasing incidence of rape, Delhi is being called the 'capital of rape'

 Priyanka Gandhi takes a holy dip in Kumbh before assuming the post of Congress General Secretary
 samachar agency ieenes ke mutabik priyanka gandhi congress adhyaksh or apane bhai rahul gandhi ke saath 4 farvari ko prayagraj main sangam main dubkee lagaayengi
 After this, she will make a formal start of her political career
 chaar farvari ko kumbh kaa doosraa shahi snaan he
 On this day there is also Mauni Amavasya
 report ke mutabik iske baad priyanka gandhi lakhanu main rahul ke saath ek saajha press conference bhi karengi
 According to the report, if for some reason Rahul Gandhi and Priyanka Gandhi Vadra are unable to bathe in the Sangam on February 4, then they will take a holy dip on February 10
 10 farvari kaa muhurt bhi khaas he
 Basant Panchami is on this day and the third is the royal bath
 mana ja rahaa he ki yah shaayad pehali baar he jab rahul gandhi or priyanka gandhi- donon sangam main snaan karenge
 Let us know that earlier in the year 2001, the then Congress President Sonia Gandhi reached the Kumbh Mela and took a holy bath
 2019 ke loksabhaa chunaav se pehle congress ne ek badi raajnneetik chaal chalate hue priyanka gandhi ko purvi uttar pradesh kaa mahasachiv niyukt kar diya he
 Eastern Uttar Pradesh has 40 to 42 seats in the Lok Sabha
 is kshetra main varanasi, gorakhpur, mughalsarai jaise ilaake aate hai, jahaan bijepi kii acchhee pakad he
 In the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, BJP won most of these seats
 priyanka gandhi ke is kadam ke raajnneetik myne nikaale ja rahe hai or ise bijepi ke dakshinpanthi vichaardhaara kaa congress dwaara jawaab bataaya ja rahaa he
 Let me tell you that in 2017, Congress President Rahul Gandhi offered prayers in many temples during the Gujarat assembly elections
 jaankaar bataate hai ki yah congress kii soft hindutv kii niti ke tahat kiya gaya tha
 Rahul's move was criticized by BJP and said that Rahul remembers temples only when the election comes
 rahul gandhi kaa mandir dauraan karnataka chunaav ke alaava haal hi main hue rajasthan, empi or chhattisgarh main bhi jari rahaa tha
 In response to repeated criticisms of the BJP, Rahul Gandhi had said that he understands Hindu religion better than the people of BJP
 rajasthan vidhansabha chunaav ke dauraan rahul gandhi ne khud ko janeudhari hindu bataaya tha
 While worshiping in a temple in Rajasthan, Rahul described his gotra as Dattatreya and Brahmin
 ek vidhayak ne rajya ke grahamantri aaraar patil se yah kahkar buudhvaar ko maharashtra vidhansabha main khalabali machaa di ki vah paanch lakh rupee main pune kii yeravada jail se ‘faraar’ ho sakate hai
 Dhule MLA Anil Gote said, "I know what happens in jails
" ek jail main main chaar saal ke liye tha
 Gote was accused in crores of rupees stamp paper scam and was lodged in Yerwada jail in the case
 gote ne pune se bijepi vidhayak maadhuri misaal dwaara prashn kaal ke dauraan pune jail main kaidiyon ko mobile phone or anya suvidhaayen avaidh tareeke se uplabdh karaae jane ke bare main poochne par yah tippanee kii
 Patil said that the process of installing CCTV and jammers in the jails is on
 gote ne hastkshep karte hue kaha ki vah jaanate hai ki jail kii chaharadivari ke peeche kya chalata he

 After this, the company has made many small major changes from the Facebook interface to the data and user policy
 ab aap apane data kii jaankaree pehle ke mukaable aasaani se paa sakate hai
 In this sequence, Facebook will now give you more information about the advertisement shown
 fasebuk ne kuch nae apadats kaa elaan kiya he
 These updates will be seen in the section Why am i seeing this ad
 iskaa makasad yugers ko zyada transperency or control dena he
 That is, if you see an advertisement on Facebook, then you can use the option Why am i seeing this ad
 ye opshan pehle bhi tha, lekin isamen kuch nae fitures aid kiye ja rahe hai
 By clicking it, you can know on what basis this advertisement is being shown to you
 yahaan aap ye bhi dekh paaenge ki aapaki dilchaspee or katigari match hui he or is vajah se ye khaas vigyaapan aapako dikhaaya ja rahaa he
 Not only this, you will also be able to see where this information has come from and who are the data brokers
 yani koun si company he jo aapaki dilchaspee ke aadhaar par aapako vigyaapan dikhaa rahi he
 Under this feature of Facebook, if you wish, you can also block the advertisement of that particular advertiser
 darasal ye feechar fasebuk ke zyada yugers ke liye phydemand sabit hoga
 Because Facebook is almost completely ad based and you are given free service so that the company can make money from advertising
 ye sabakuch fasebuk aapaki sahmati ke saath karata he jo aap fasebuk acount banaate vakt dete hai
 Facebook has added a new option under the Ad preference section
 ye nayaa teb Advertisers and business kaa he
 Under this, you will get to know some interesting things which will be related to you
 fasebuk ke is section main ja kar aap ye dekh sakenge ki koun sa third party data brokar aapaki personal dilchaspee ke aadhaar par yahaan aapako list kar rahaa he
 To put it simply, if you buy something from a grocery store and the list of customers' email ID has been uploaded from that store and it is being used for the target ad on Facebook
 isse aapako ye andaja ho jayega ki aapkaa data fasebuk par kahaan se aa rahaa he, iskaa kya yuj ho rahaa he or koun si companiyaan aapaki dilchaspee ke hisaab se yahaan vigyaapan de rahe hai
 Yes, one thing to keep in mind that you can block an advertisement on behalf of a particular third party data broker, but there is no option to block the ad completely nor can it happen in future
 kam se kam jab tak fasebuk free he
 However, if you do not want some third party data broker to advertise to you, you can go to Facebook's settings and tap on Ad preferences here

 If work is only the scale, then its highest level is that the one who will not live up to the task will be out
 uskaa ucchtam str yah nahin he ki jiskaa kaam karaab hoga, use doosraa mantralay milegaa
 As soon as memory was removed, the opposing part of social media erupted
 isamen koi shaq nahin ki smriti ko lekar ek tabaqa khundak main rahata he, party ke bheetar bhi or party ke baahar bhi
 Everyone started swinging
 pichley do saal main smriti party or sarkaar kii aakraamak senapati bani hui thim
 The political talents of Smriti were praised, their speeches were praised, the antagonists ate
 sangh smriti ko apana pratik mantri maanata tha
 While standing in Parliament, devotees used to think on social media, Sachin Tendulkar has come in the slog-over
 mangalvaar raat ke baad ek jatke main saare vishleshan badal gaye
 The stature of memory has been shortened
 unka kaam acha nahin rahaa, isliye modi ne unhen apni pasand suchi se baahar kar diya
 All those who discussed the cabinet, who were avoiding the open criticism of the Prime Minister by saying 'jumbo' and 'electoral machinery', now got an opportunity to praise Modi
 twit karne lage ki modi sirf kaam pasand karte hai, unka koi pasandida nahin hota he
 If there is such a keen eye on work, then tell me why sir, she remained in this ministry for two years
 
 
 ? jabaki irani ke kai faisalon kii aalochana ho rahi thi or vivaad bhi ho rahe the
 For two years, it was never felt that the party and the Prime Minister were not happy with Smriti Irani's performance
 pradarshan kii yah koun-si monitering hui ki kathith rup se ek karaab mantri ko hataane main do saal lag gaye
 The discussions in which the brand Modi was weakening, now started blossoming in the same discussions
 ek faisale se cabinet vistaar ke hero pradhanmantri ban gaye or jo abhi tak cabinet kii sabase badi heroin thim, unhen khalanayika bana diya gaya
 Whereas the same debater once praised Smriti Irani, because then she was the Minister of Human Resources and confidant of the Prime Minister
 smriti irani ke liye bhi sabak he
 He has to prove again that he is not important because of the post, he is due to talent
 captain ne sirf ballebaazi kram main badlaav kiya he
 Otherwise, even the spokespersons of the party did not understand how to defend against so many state ministers
 lihaaza ve apni hi sarkaar kii pole kholane lage
 Started speaking that so many ministers of state are made for the promotion of work, not for work
 party ne sarkari karche par prachaar gaadi rakh liye hai
 Nobody was able to defend properly
 ab sabko nayaa hathiyaar mil gaya
 Nobody is better than Modi
 yah koun-si nai kaaryastylee he ki sarkari kharche par prachaar karne ke liye rajyamantri bhare ja rahe hai
 Nobody is telling what are the tasks of the ministers of state
 vaise to yah bhi kaha jaataa he ki jab kaabina mantriyon ke paas kaam nahin, to rajyamantri ko puch koun rahaa he
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi goes two steps ahead of his opponents and critics
 unke aalochakon kii ek kubi he
 They start swinging in criticism
 tabhi modi kuch aisa karte hai ki unhen lagata he kisi ne jhatka de diya
 Modi changed Irani's ministry and raised his imprint and credibility
 cabinet kaa vistaar or pherbadal ab modi style kii muhar kaa ek or dastauez bataaya ja rahaa he, jiske bare main pradhanmantri khud media se kah rahe the ki yah badlaav nahin, vistaar he
 Why said this, who asked all this
 agar smriti ko karaab pradarshan ke kaaran hataaya gaya to prakaash jaavdekar ko kyon hataaya gaya
 
 
 The There was a lot of applause when he was sworn in as the only cabinet minister to be promoted
 vaise aachaar-vyavhaar main prakaash ji kaiyon se behatar netaa hai, magar jis paryaavaran mantralay main unke behatar kaam ke liye cabinet mantri banaaya gaya, vahaan se hataaya kyon gaya
 When a good minister gets hold of himself in two years, the decision to remove him becomes an example of performance politics
 piyush goyal ke pramot hone kii koob charchaa ho rahi thi, nahin hue
 But when news of the reshuffle came, the number of his departments was increased
 yah pramotion kii koun-si style he

 ? agar pradhanmantri pradarshan ko ziddi dhun kii str tak pasand karte hai to abhi tak ek sthaayee kanoon mantri kyon nahin khoj sake
 
 
 The The law ministry's comment is on whose style of work
 
 
 ? sadanand gauda kaa agar kanoon mantri ke rup main kaam acha nahin tha to kis daleel se unhen cabinet main rakhaa gaya he
 
 
 The zaahir he, sakht sawaalon se bachane ke liye mantriyon ke hisaab se tark gadhe ja rahe hai
 Everybody got busy in provoking anger about Smriti Irani
 pradhanmantri ne apni chhavi ke liye apane sabase pyaare mantri ko daanv par laga diya yaa vaaqai vah mantri naakaara thim, iskaa faisalaa itihaas karegaa, kyonki vartmaan smriti irani se chidhata he
 Irritation is not a correct assessment
 jaise hi khabar aegi ki smriti kahin kii mukhyamantri kii ummidavaar hai, phir se yahi charchaakaar unki khubiyaan bataane lagenge
 The Ministry of Rural Development is bigger than the Ministry of Human Resources
 iske mantri choudhary virendra singh ko hataakar chote-se mantralay main bhej diya gaya
 It is not even discussed anywhere
 
 
 ? kya virendra singh bhi fel hue hai
